Hong Kong's Wartime Preparations Amidst the Turmoil: Increasing Combat Personnel and Expanding the Scope of Conscription

Hong Kong Correspondence: Since the expansion of the European war situation, the Hong Kong authorities have become increasingly rigorous in their wartime preparations. Although the Governor of Hong Kong, Sir Geoffry Northcote, has left Hong Kong on vacation last month, it is said that he consulted with the Singapore authorities when he passed through Singapore to discuss the connection between Singapore and Hong Kong to facilitate military operations. He also decided to implement the opening of war taxes in Hong Kong before leaving Hong Kong. Therefore, the War Tax Bureau has recently notified major commercial firms to report their business accounts for last year within a month. Those who conceal or falsely report figures to underreport after the deadline will be charged with violating the War Tax Act. This shows one aspect of the preparations.

Strengthening Strength: Establishing a Compulsory Military Service Bureau

Regarding strength, the Hong Kong authorities are actively seeking to increase combat personnel. Therefore, the scope of conscription has been expanded, and combat supplementary regiments have been added. In addition to the regular army, Hong Kong usually has naval and land volunteer forces, which are voluntary in nature, and their organization and equipment are comparable to the regular army. In the past three years, due to the many events in Europe, they have been actively expanding and intensifying training. People of various nationalities, including Chinese, English, Portuguese, and Indian, have participated, with the English being the most numerous. The Army Volunteer Force has a total of six battalions of high-射炮 anti-aircraft gun, machine gun, and rifle units. The Navy Volunteer Force has multiple patrol boats. Recently, ships coming and going to the Hong Kong port have been rented for further training. A unit has been dispatched to patrol the port and perform guard duties. As for the British in Hong Kong, they had previously received instructions from London to enlist in Hong Kong. Therefore, the Hong Kong authorities have established a compulsory military service bureau to review the British men of conscription age residing in Hong Kong and Shanghai. In addition to those who have already joined the volunteer army, the rest will be assigned to the combat ranks of the navy and army. Therefore, many British expatriates in Shanghai have also come to Hong Kong to enlist. Those who do not want to join the combat team due to their jobs or circumstances must provide sufficient reasons and be approved by the compulsory military service tribunal, then they can be assigned to the guarding posts and sentry of the Army Volunteer Force to be mobilized temporarily. Previously, the military service tribunal ordered 350 people to take on this task. However, the Hong Kong authorities believe that the Hong Kong environment urgently needs to increase the wartime manpower source. Therefore, it was decided to select the patrol posts and incorporate them into the combat supplementary regiment to make them enlist in training and combat. It is also heard that 120 people have been selected.

Inspecting Ships: Defenses are Extremely Tight

As for the Hong Kong sea port, under the management of the naval authorities, it is sealed off at any time, inspecting ships entering and exiting the port, and dispatching speedboats to sail outside the port to patrol back and forth, so as to make the port and sea defense perfect. In addition, the air defense drill has recently been held twice. According to the statement issued by Mr. Speicher, the Director of Air Defense, the exercise results are still good. The air defense rescue team is also working hard to learn fire fighting techniques, and their results are also very good. After Italy announced its participation in the European War, the Hong Kong government immediately dispatched a special detective team to the residences and shops of Italian expatriates to monitor the Italian expatriates. The disposal method is the same as the disposal of German and Austrian expatriates in September last year. However, under special circumstances, it is exempted from being sent to concentration camps with the special permission of the Hong Kong government, and only police officers monitor their actions. The Italian consulate has stopped working immediately. As for Italian shipping companies, the Italian staff is monitored by a special detective team. The Chinese staff is dismissed after being interrogated, leaving only servants and Chinese and British detectives to guard. The remaining Italian church missionaries and nuns are specially allowed to maintain the status quo temporarily. However, the property kept by the priests and nuns in Hong Kong must not be moved. It can be said that the disposal is going smoothly.

The Zhe-Gan Railway Extends to Ganzhou and Construction Begins at the Beginning of the Month

Nancheng Correspondence: The Zhe-Gan Railway from Guixi to Ganzhou, which connects the major arteries of the southeast and southwest, planned to build a branch road in Ganzhou with the light rail unloaded when the Zhe-Gan Railway converted the light rail from Xiaoshan to Yushan to heavy rail in 1936. At that time, two lines were selected: one from Zhangshu along the Gan River to Ganzhou, and the other from the intersection of the Beijing-Gan and Zhe-Gan lines in Guixi through eastern Gan to Ganzhou. Although both lines have been surveyed, they failed due to various reasons. Now the authorities have decided to complete this road in the shortest possible time. It is found that this line crosses Yuqi from Guixi and crosses the Xujiang River in Nancheng, southward to Nanfeng, Guangchang, Ningdu, and reaches Ganzhou. It is about 300 kilometers long. The survey has already been completed and civil workers will be recruited to build in sections. Construction is scheduled to begin on July 1 and be completed by the end of the year. After this road is successful, it can be connected to the Yue-Gui and Yue-Han lines from Ganzhou to Shaoguan, serving as a major artery connecting the southeast and southwest.

Zhejiang Province Convenes a Meeting to Discuss Relief for the Rice Shortage: 200 People Starve to Death in Shaoxing Every Day

Yongkang Correspondence: The Zhejiang Provincial Grain Management Office learned that the rice shortage in the counties under Shaoxing is severe, the price of rice in Shaoxing is exceptionally high, and the black market price has risen to over 100 yuan per stone.

The average number of people starving to death reaches 200 per day, and the autumn harvest is still far away. The source of Gan rice is also gradually decreasing. In order to understand the grain demand figures of the grain-deficient counties so as to find ways to provide relief, a provincial grain conference was specially convened in Yongkang at 3 pm on the 12th. More than one hundred people attended, including commissioners of various districts, county heads of various counties, and local gentry. Provincial party and government committees also participated, and Huang Shaohong personally presided over the meeting. The content of the discussion included (1) sources of rice, (2) improving grain management methods, (3) increasing the purchase price of grain-surplus counties, (4) strictly practicing thrift and adjusting distribution, (5) granary preparations, and (6) general survey of grain prices. All representatives believed that they were essential and must be implemented. The government formulated measures for various counties to follow. If representatives have any opinions, they can submit them in writing within ten days. Representatives from the counties under Ningbo proposed that the procedures for collecting export certificates should be used to subsidize grain, which should be handled by each county according to local conditions. Deng Ren, the magistrate of Shaoxing County, made a temporary motion, requesting the provincial government to transport grain to Shaoxing as soon as possible to meet the needs of the military and the people and maintain local stability. Zhu Huiqing, deputy director of the Grain Management Office, replied that 70,000 dan of rice had been purchased to relieve the rice shortage in Shaoxing and was being shipped successively to be properly distributed for various counties to purchase and transport, and the transportation problem would be borne jointly by the various counties. Chairman Huang also instructed the county heads to pay attention to the grain shortage in the coming year, find ways to plant arable land, plant as much miscellaneous grain as possible, and promote thrift, and implement them effectively after returning to office. The provincial government also resolved to allocate 50,000 yuan and allocate another 30,000 yuan from the grain accumulation funds in Shaoxing to subsidize the economic porridge factory expenses in Shaoxing County.

The Initial Situation of the European War (VII)

— Shu Di

On the eve of the declaration of war on Germany by Britain and France when the German-Polish war broke out, Franco broadcasted the following: "I appeal to the sense of responsibility and goodwill of all countries and governments, hoping to use their efforts as much as possible to localize this war (referring to the German-Polish war - author's note). The expansion of a war will inevitably cause a profound and irreparable disruption of the world economy, countless losses of world resources, paralyze world trade, and give the general public a severe blow to the standard of living. If this war is further expanded, then the seeds of a bigger war in the future will be sown."

This passage truly expresses Spain's intentions. First, she admits that the German-Polish war is justified; second, she opposes the "expansion" of the war by Britain and France; if Britain and France declare war on Germany, then they are the instigators of disrupting the world's economic life; and, incidentally, she gives Britain and France a threat that Spain may participate.

(6) Other Countries Declaring "Neutrality" (September 20)

The Second European War has been going on for exactly twenty days since the curtain was raised on the German-Polish War on September 1. In addition to the positions of the various countries that have already been described above in this war, the attitudes of the remaining countries are also an indispensable part of understanding this decisive picture of the European war situation. Here, I will first give them a temporary general classification.

The European political units left over from the last European war are thirty-five: England, Italy, Sweden, Norway, Denmark, the Netherlands, Belgium, Hungary, Romania, Yugoslavia, Bulgaria, Albania, Iceland, France, Germany, Poland, Finland, Estonia, Latvia, Lithuania, Czechoslovakia, Austria, Switzerland, Greece, Spain, Portugal, Turkey, San Marino, Andorra, the Soviet Union, Luxembourg, Monaco, Liechtenstein, the Irish Free State, and the Free City of Danzig.

However, before this war broke out, Czechoslovakia, Austria, and Albania, three countries had already been eliminated.

The Free City of Danzig was the fuse for Germany's invasion of Poland. The participants in the war were Germany on one side and Britain, France, and Poland on the other. A total of four countries. The Soviet Union's position is different from any country and has special significance.

Italy declared "non-participation in the war," but it is clear that she is an ally of Germany; Spain declared "neutrality," but in attitude, she is biased towards Germany. - These two countries are one type.

Turkey declared "loyalty" to the British and French alliance treaties, but did not participate in the war; Romania, in fact, is equal to an ally of Britain and France, but declared "neutrality." - These two countries are another type.

After removing the above thirteen political units, there are twenty-two political units remaining in Europe. Among them, there are two that have not yet formally declared "neutrality." - Hungary, Greece.

The rest have all declared so-called "neutrality" one after another. Here are the attitudes of three of the more important countries among them.

Belgium - Belgium, which suffered from the misfortune of being caught in the crossfire in the last European war, is once again bearing the brunt. Theoretically, for strategic reasons, the belligerent countries that drag her into the vortex are more likely to be Germany. Therefore, starting from this assumption, her defenses are entirely facing the German side. However, in fact, Britain and France, which subjectively hope that she will join the vortex, are not inferior to Germany, because they estimate that if Belgium does not join, then it will be, if she joins, it must be on the side of Britain and France, that means to say, the British and French side can immediately have another ally. Therefore, recently the propaganda of Britain and France and the propaganda of Germany have become two interesting contrasts. Germany is trying its best to deny any intention to invade Belgium. On the contrary, it says that Britain and France want to violate her neutrality; at the same time, it is doing its best to encourage her to resist. Following that, it released a threat: "If Belgium acquiesces in Britain and France destroying her neutrality, then Germany also has the right to take convenient action and no longer has any obligation to respect her neutrality." On the British and French side, they are reminding her of the lessons of the last European war every day, encouraging her to prepare for the German invasion, and saying: "Belgium can rest assured that on the first day the German army sets foot on Belgian territory, the British and French allied forces will be able to come to the rescue immediately." However, standing on Belgium's position, she has no ambition to expand her territory, nor does she want to offer her territory as someone else's battlefield. Therefore, her most advantageous path is to be a truly "neutral" to the end. Therefore, the propaganda and pressure from both sides of the belligerent countries are things that make her "painful." When Britain, France and Germany declared war, Belgium also immediately issued a general mobilization order nationwide, not to prepare to join any side to fight, but indeed to prepare to "guarantee its own neutrality." Education News

Zhejiang Province Cultivates Technical Personnel: Plans to Quickly Establish Vocational Schools at All Levels; Each County Can Set Up Junior Vocational Schools at its Discretion

(Fangyan Correspondence) Zhejiang Province has always attached great importance to the development of vocational education. Recently, in view of the urgent need for various technical personnel during the wartime, it is even more necessary to actively promote it. It has been decided to follow the following three principles: (1) Establish vocational schools at all levels to cultivate young people's knowledge of life and production skills to increase social wealth and enrich people's livelihoods; (2) Vocational schools at all levels should cultivate senior talents in various fields and improve inherent products; (3) Vocational supplementary education should be promoted at the same time. A detailed implementation method and schedule are formulated in the three-year administration plan, as follows:

Methods

(1) Establish a provincial junior textile vocational school to cultivate talents to improve the textile industry; (2) Establish a provincial senior commercial vocational school to cultivate accounting, finance and business talents; (3) Establish a provincial junior agricultural vocational school to cultivate talents to improve the province's specialties; (4) Establish a provincial senior industrial vocational school to cultivate talents for the processing and manufacturing of the province's specialties; (5) Establish a provincial junior industrial vocational school to cultivate talents to improve papermaking; (6) Establish a provincial senior applied chemistry vocational school to cultivate talents for the improvement and manufacturing of daily necessities; (7) Each county should investigate and consider the actual needs of local occupations, and can set up county-level junior vocational schools to train various primary vocational technical talents to improve various local products; (8) Regarding vocational supplementary education, the province will designate the Provincial Yingshi University College of Agriculture, Engineering and Medicine, Provincial Hangzhou Sericulture Vocational School, Ningbo Senior Industrial Vocational School, Jinhua Experimental Agricultural Vocational School, Xianghu Township Teacher, Wenzhou Township Teacher, Temporary United High School Normal School and other ten colleges and universities to attach employee training classes or vocational supplementary classes. The county-run schools will designate counties with provincial and county financial divisions to supervise and universally run them.

Schedule

(1) In the first year, establish a provincial junior textile and senior commercial vocational school; in the second year, establish a provincial junior agricultural and senior industrial school; in the third year, establish a provincial junior industrial vocational school and a senior applied chemistry vocational school; (2) Seven items will be supervised by the province to be handled in stages based on the actual situation of each county; (3) For vocational supplementary education, the province will first try it out in the designated provincial ten colleges and universities in the first year, and in the second and third years, it will find ways to extend it to other provincial schools to handle them separately. County-run schools will be handled according to the progress of county-run junior vocational schools.

Guangxi Province Implements the National Education Plan

(Guilin, 24th) The Ministry of Education telegraphed the provincial government that the implementation of national education in Guangxi has been tentatively formulated within the overall plan and will be completed within three years. In the first year, 1,100 central schools and 6,000 national schools will be converted, and 7,100 teachers will be trained in the short term. In the second year, 1,200 central schools and 7,000 national schools will be converted, and 8,200 teachers will be trained in the short term. In the third year, 8,000 national schools will be converted, and 8,000 teachers will be trained in the short term. The subsidy fees are included in the overall budget, 1,384,500 yuan in the first year, 2,664,000 yuan in the second year, 3,156,000 yuan in the third year, 2,796,000 yuan in the fourth year, and 2,097,000 yuan in the fifth year. The original five-year plan of Guangxi should be revised and reported for approval after the overall plan budget is approved.

Key Points of the Regulations of the Three Principles of the People Education Research Association (Continued from yesterday)

(6) Research Groups: According to the instructions of the Central Committee, they are divided into the following nine groups. If necessary, they can be submitted to the Central Committee for approval to increase or decrease them. A. National Issue Group, B. Democratic Issue Group, C. Local Autonomy Issue Group, D. Administrative Agency Issue Group, E. Land Issue Group, F. Capital Issue Group, G. Economic Construction Issue Group, H. Education Issue Group, I. Ethics Issue Group.

(7) Research Methods: A. Members must identify at least one group for research when joining the association and must not exceed three groups at most. B. Research is conducted through correspondence at ordinary times, and research is conducted in a gathering during the summer vacation. The duration of the gathering research shall not be less than four weeks. C. During the gathering period, research is conducted by the following methods: Zǐ: Answering the outline: The research department will draft a question outline and a list of reference books for each group and send them to each member for reading and research, and engage in answering them. Chǒu: Discussion meetings: There are two types: group discussions and group discussions. The group discussion is chaired by the instructor of each group, and the group discussion is chaired by the president or vice president, and the instructors of each group participate in the guidance. Yín: Lecture meetings: invite the highest party and government authorities, instructors of the association, and comrades who have rich research on the Three Principles of the People to serve as them.

(8) Members who participate in the gathering research, in addition to researching various issues, must also write a thesis after the end of the gathering research and submit it to the research association (the topic must be approved by the instructor). Those who pass the review will be given a certificate of qualification.

(9) Appointment of Members: Members who have a certificate of qualification will be selected by the Ministry of Education and sent to various colleges and universities for employment, with the same treatment as other full-time teachers, and should also serve as tutors.

(10) Party doctrine teachers currently employed in colleges or higher who do not participate in the research within one year of the establishment of the research association will be suspended from their qualifications to teach the Three Principles of the People.

(11) Member Treatment: Travel expenses, board and lodging during the gathering research period will be provided by the association. Those who are currently unemployed will also be given allowances.

(12) Research Association Publications: A. A periodical publication, B. An outline for lecturing on the Three Principles of the People must be approved by the instructor and used as the standard for the Three Principles of the People course in colleges or higher, C. Teaching materials for the Three Principles of the People, compiled according to the outline for lecturing, D. A series of books on the Three Principles of the People, reference materials for lecturing on the Three Principles of the People.

(13) Research Association Expenses: Submitted separately.

School News

Li Xin Accounting Supplementary School: The Municipal Li Xin Accounting Supplementary School originally had night school, morning school, Sunday school, and correspondence school, etc. Although the talents trained in each period are already considerable, in order to achieve the original purpose of providing students with study in their spare time, each semester can only study one or two tax courses, which takes a long time, and is often too impatient for those who have not yet been employed and are eager to quickly become a good accounting talent. Therefore, it was decided to add one class each in the middle school group and university group intensive courses in the next semester. It is stipulated that there will be 20 hours of class per week, and various necessary courses such as elementary accounting, advanced accounting, cost accounting, bank accounting, government accounting, and auditing will be completed in two semesters, so as to prepare students graduating from middle school and university general subjects or those with equivalent qualifications to learn a skill in the shortest possible time to facilitate those who are about to be employed.

Finance: Chinese Merchants Selling Foreign Exchange En Masse

In yesterday's foreign exchange market, HSBC's listed prices remained unchanged. The underground market for British and American currencies showed a persistent downward trend, especially the US dollar today, which was particularly weak. This was mainly due to a sharp rise of more than 1 jiao and 3 fen in the exchange rate between British and American currencies in the early morning. Trading was lively throughout the day, with Chinese banks such as Huaqiao and Shanghai selling foreign exchange en masse, which was the main reason for the weakening. However, there were no reports of Chinese speculators entering or leaving the market, resulting in a shortage of scalpers. The strongest US dollar in the morning was 6.125 yuan, with the closing price remaining stable. In the afternoon, the market became increasingly rigid. Chinese banks quoted 6.125 yuan and 6 yuan for six-seven month swaps, indicating a discount of 0.125 yuan. Furthermore, the Japanese Yokohama Specie Bank (Y.S.K.) also sought to sell a considerable amount of spot US dollars, with the price reaching 6.15625 yuan at one point. However, American banks absorbed a significant amount, causing the price to slightly recover after the weakening. As a result, the closing prices were 3 shillings 9.6875 pence for British gold and 6.09375 yuan for the US dollar. Compared to the closing prices last Saturday, British gold remained unchanged, while the US dollar rose sharply by 0.125 yuan. Futures also remained firm.

The evening closing prices for Siam No. 2 and Tribute No. 2 rice were only around 61 yuan, with Bank Warehouse slightly squeezed to 60.034 yuan, and a few small traders in a hurry to sell even lowering their prices to below 60 yuan, at 59.8 yuan. Early market prices for recycled Siam No. 2 18-bag rice were 67 yuan, down 1.5 yuan from Saturday, and then ranged from 67.5 yuan to 68 yuan, but there was also a lack of demand in the evening market. The total number of futures recycled throughout the day was 250 tons, and there were 8,000 bags in stock.

Also, according to news, foreign rice continued to arrive in Shanghai. The Taikoo Company's Guangdong ship arrived in Shanghai last Saturday, transporting 20,008 bags from Hong Kong, which were unloaded yesterday. The company's Xinjiang ship also arrived on the 23rd, also carrying 11,784 bags from Hong Kong, which were docked at the company's wharf in Pudong for unloading. (Zu)

Although the arrival of Japonica and Glutinous national rice was continuous, it was not large, only nearly 1,000 bags in total. Due to the heavy rain, the underground market for Japonica rice was still strong, and it was not affected by foreign rice or rainfall. There were still many transactions, and the selling price was similar to the previous price. Changbang's special clear Japonica rice was 75 yuan, Su Kun and Changzhou Japonica rice were 73-74 yuan, Qingsi's special thin rice was 73-74 yuan, large-grain rice was 71-72 yuan, and old rice was 70 yuan. Nangang's early rice was 69 yuan. The sales market for Glutinous rice turned inferior, and the situation was not as firm as before, with the price depreciating by about half a yuan. Early Kimli special yuan rice was 60 yuan, Dan Chang Baiyuan rice was 58-59 yuan, and Jiangbei goods were around 57 yuan.

The Wuxi Rice Milling Industry Association held a meeting on the 20th and decided to advise fellow traders to sell their stocks as much as possible to meet the market demand, and also agreed on a limited price of 20.5 yuan per dan for Japonica rice, 40 yuan per shi for coarse Japonica rice, and 43 yuan for white Japonica rice, and not to increase the price again, in order to maintain the people's food supply. Each rice factory must be responsible for automatically refusing large-scale purchases by certain merchants and transporting them out of the country. If anyone violates the agreement, the industry's transactions will be suspended, and all factories and businesses will comply with the agreement with full stamps. (Zhi)

Noodles Rise by Half a Yuan

Flour: The plate of Factory No. 2 flour yesterday rose from 13.8 yuan to 14.3 yuan, adding half a yuan steeper than before. The reason for the rise was that the Chinese factories were affected by the obstruction of new wheat, and the raw materials were about to run out, and there was a situation where there was no goods to supply. Remedial measures have been discussed and agreed upon, and it has been resolved that all guest traders and hoarders will stop selling, and the normal supply will be provided according to the current actual sales volume of this street. Therefore, the factory plate will be actually increased. However, with the current high price of rice, the sales volume in this street is increasing day by day, and the direct distribution by the factory is no less than 10,000 bags. Recycled goods are even more profitable due to the increase in the factory plate. The asking price for Lao Che Pi is 15 yuan, and the asking price for Lu Pao Che and Tian Zhu and other flours is 17 yuan, but they are not formal market prices.

Also, it has been found that since the price of rice has been expensive, flour has attracted the attention of the general public, and the factory's production is limited, and there is a situation where they are unable to meet the demand. It is heard that Tianjin has ordered more than 100,000 bags of Australian flour and foreign flour, and local grain merchants have also ordered foreign flour. It is said that the Tianjin side has ordered Australian flour, and the local side has ordered American flour, estimated at more than 50,000 bags, and the price is 15.5 yuan, which is considered cheap.

Wheat: Yesterday's wheat supply still failed to return to normal, and the Japanese factories have repeatedly received supplies, and their situation is special and cannot be compared with the same day, while the Chinese factories, in view of the current harsh environment, cannot directly purchase from the producing areas, and have no choice but to release prices and start purchasing from grain merchants, businesses, and a certain party. It is heard that yesterday, Fufeng Factory received more than 500 bags of new wheat from Wuhu and Jiangbei, priced at 24.3 yuan to 24 yuan.

Silk & Tea: Tin Cocoon Merchants Are Scams: Received Cocoon from Farmers; Did Not Send Money to Farmers

There are more than 300 large and small cocoon shops in the three counties of Xiwu and Cheng, most of which collect cocoons on behalf of the "China Central Company." At that time, a contract was established to falsely establish a fresh cocoon price list. If the orchid price rose and fell, it would be calculated according to the report. At the time of payment, except for a small amount of deposit paid first at the time of ordering, the rest will be paid in silver when the dry cocoons are transported to the city. At the time of weighing, due to the special circumstances, the cocoon shops still issued joint tickets as in the previous year, and the date of distribution was announced, stating that the dry cocoons were transported to the city, received the money, and returned home to pay. Now that most of the dry cocoons have been transported to the city, each line has requested the "China Central Company" to pay and settle accounts as agreed. The issue of cocoon prices has not yet been settled, and there are tens of thousands of households in the countryside who hold joint tickets, because cash has not yet been received, and they have been sitting and demanding money from the cocoon shops. The main cocoon shops cannot deal with this situation, and they have gathered in Wuxi to discuss and negotiate with the "China Central Company." If a solution is not quickly sought, there will still be dry cocoons left in the countryside, and it will be difficult to transport them to the city. In this case, the farmers' hard work of raising silkworms will be in vain. (Liang)

Wuxi Silk Comes to Shanghai: Taxed 300 Yuan: The Industry Seeks Countermeasures

Although the Wuxi silk coming to Shanghai has not actually been subjected to a donation of 12%, it has been greatly restricted. Several pieces of silk have already obtained a transfer certificate (the so-called pass), which requires a pass fee of 300 yuan in legal tender per dan. After July, a special donation of nearly 600 yuan will be required. Yesterday, the silk factory industry association specially convened a meeting to seek countermeasures.

Metals After the Price of Foreign Nails Fell, New Coiled Wire Followed

The new coiled wire market has been in a slump since the price of foreign nails fell. Recently, the situation in Vietnam and southern China has become increasingly serious, and merchants there have no time to purchase goods. The only large sales market for foreign nails is the islands of Southeast Asia and the major commercial ports of the South China Sea. Now that the situation has greatly changed, there are no goods to be shipped for foreign nails, and the various merchant groups are also unwilling to purchase them. Therefore, the foreign nail market situation has been severely impacted. Although the local construction industry and retail buyers occasionally make purchases, the volume is small. Therefore, the trend in the nail market is very poor, and the price has fallen from 65.5 yuan to around 60 yuan, causing the new coiled wire market price to follow suit. Yesterday, the market price was 55 yuan per dan (unit of weight), also falling by 4 yuan or so.

French Defense Force and Police Yesterday Evacuated Xujiahui; Japan-puppet Regime and French Side Reached an Agreement Through Negotiations; General Order Within the Town is Still Considered Stable

Before the war, Xujiahui Town in western Shanghai was under the jurisdiction of the municipal government. After the westward retreat of the national army, the French Concession authorities, because the area had a refugee zone and because the French Catholic Church owned a great deal of property in the area, dispatched troops to be stationed there and temporarily set up a police station at the intersection of Ciyou Road and Huizhan Street in the town. They distributed posts at important locations to maintain order, under the administration of the French Concession. For more than two years, they lived in peace. Moreover, because the location was remote and there were not many residents, many factories and institutions moved there during the time when the concession was crowded with people. Therefore, the area actually had the function of regulating the population in the concession, which indirectly helped maintain law and order in the concession. However, the Japan-puppet regime's military police suddenly invaded the area the day before yesterday, causing rumors to arise and people to panic. The situation was quite tense. As seen in yesterday's newspaper, according to further investigation, the French Concession authorities have reached a compromise with the Japan-puppet regime, and starting from 1:00 AM this morning, the area will be handed over to the Japan-puppet regime. The details are recorded below:

Brewing for a Long Time, Agreement Recently Reached

Recently, the Japan-puppet side, using the excuse that there were no more refugees in the area, demanded that the French side withdraw the defense force and police station. It is reported that this negotiation has been conducted between the French Concession authorities and the puppet "municipal government" for many days. Until yesterday, it was completely resolved. The French side, due to the harsh environment and unwillingness to cause disputes, expressed concessions and, starting from 12:00 last night, withdrew the defense force and police station to within the concession. Starting from 1:00 AM this morning, it was handed over to the Japan-puppet side to take over. According to the Japanese military spokesman at a reception for reporters last night, he also admitted that "this issue will be resolved today (i.e., tomorrow)," but he was unwilling to release the details. However, the French Concession authorities and the Japanese embassy spokesman neither confirmed nor denied it.

Residents Hearing the News, Moved One After Another

Since the Japan-puppet regime's military police invaded the area the day before yesterday, yesterday morning, the Japanese army held exercises nearby again. The general residents, because they were worried about what kind of situation would arise, were greatly panicked and moved one after another. Although it rained heavily yesterday afternoon, the number of people moving actually increased. On the various roads in Xujiahui, boxes and vehicles were connected endlessly, all soaked in rainwater. The general residents, supporting the old and carrying the young, all fled towards the concession, whispering to each other, showing a look of panic. As for the temporary police station of the French Concession in the area, after moving the documents and equipment out all night the day before yesterday, only empty houses remained yesterday.

Iron Wire Erected at the Border

The intersection of Haig Road, Avenue Petain, and Xujiahui Road has always been the only thoroughfare between Xujiahui Town and the French Concession. Yesterday, the area was erected with barbed wire by the Japan-puppet regime's military police, leaving only a five-foot-long gap for the entry and exit of trams and pedestrians. However, there were no Japan-puppet personnel stationed at the gap yesterday, so residents were still able to enter and exit freely. As for Haig Road, there were originally two lines of barbed wire, one adjacent to the Chinese area and one in the middle of the concession, which was the road. Now, the barbed wire adjacent to the Chinese area has been completely removed by the Japan-puppet personnel, and even the wooden poles have been pulled out.

Observatory Still Working as Usual

The Xujiahui Observatory in the Xujiahui area is an important place for reporting and observing weather in the Far East. In the future, when all the French police detectives are withdrawn, the work of the observatory is of great concern to the shipping industry. According to inquiries, the observatory worked as usual yesterday and will not be suspended in the future. The weather station and other facilities there cannot be moved, and it has been decided to continue working at the original location. In addition, the Xujiahui Catholic Church, seminary, monastery, and bishop's residence are also not preparing to move.

Situation in the Town Still Considered Peaceful

Yesterday, Japanese military trucks and Japan-puppet military police came and went in Xujiahui Town from time to time. Although many residents were uneasy, the general order was still considered stable. Xuhui Middle School, Xuhui Girls' High School, Qiming Girls' High School, and other schools all had classes as usual yesterday. The Xujiahui French Catholic Church is still safe, and most shops are also open for business as usual. However, at about 2:00 PM yesterday, when it was raining heavily, the extremely long bamboo fence of the Xuhui shelter was suddenly completely demolished by hundreds of poor people and taken back for fuel. Although the Chinese police were stationed beside them, they only watched to avoid causing trouble.

Security Strengthened in the Border Area of the Concession

In order to maintain the tranquility of the western district, the French Concession police authorities specially dispatched a large number of detectives yesterday, distributed at the intersections of Haig Road leading into the concession, and the inspection of pedestrians and vehicles was very strict. At the end of Xujiahui Road, which was blocked by barbed wire by the Japan-puppet regime, there was an armored vehicle and many detectives stationed at the gap, with extremely tight defenses. French police and Annamite police were rarely found in Xujiahui Town yesterday, but White Russian and Chinese police were still maintaining order in various places in the town. There was a rumor locally that there would be a retreat last night, but it could not be confirmed.

Italian Consul Going North; Danish Consul Temporarily Serves as Leader of the Consular Corps

The English-language China Press reported that the Italian Consul General in Shanghai and leader of the Consular Corps in this city, Mr. Niro, is scheduled to leave Shanghai on the 25th for a three-week vacation in Beidaihe. The Danish Consul General in Shanghai, Mr. Hill, will temporarily serve as the leader of the Consular Corps. The post of Italian Consul General will be temporarily held by Mr. Leibeks, an official of the Italian Consulate's court, until Mr. Niro returns to office.

The Situation of Refugees Awaiting Repatriation in Nanshi is Miserable; Charitable Lottery Tickets are Issued as Usual

The refugees in the Nanshi Refugee Zone, except for the old and weak who were transferred to the Xin Puyu Hall for accommodation, will all be given a month's worth of alms at the end of this month and repatriated. The Rehabilitation Committee of the District has already announced this to all the refugees in the district. It is reported that there are mostly women and children among the refugees in the district, mostly poor households from the suburbs of Shanghai and those who have lived in Nanshi for a long time. One-fifth of the refugees are from distant places. Since Father Jacquinot left Shanghai and the refugee zone is preparing to close, all the refugees in the district feel deeply at a loss, especially the refugees from distant places, who have a feeling of not knowing where to turn. The miserable situation is particularly pitiful. The Charity Lottery, which is the only economic source for the refugee zone, has been decided by the company authorities not to be suspended due to the closure of the refugee zone, because two or three charitable organizations are currently relying on the surplus funds from the lottery for subsidies. At the same time, in these extraordinary times, when the municipal finances are difficult, funds are needed for street beggars and homeless refugees to ensure their well-being. Therefore, it has been decided to continue issuing and making appropriate allocations to increase local public welfare.

Converting Tribute Rice from Saigon to Hong Kong, then Shipping to Shanghai; Cutting off Transportation is Absolutely Not True; Food Committee to Hold Important Meeting Today

The Food Committee established by the Municipal Council is scheduled to hold a committee meeting at 2:15 PM today. The members of the committee are Marshall (Chairman), Iveley, Grand, Hongk, Hedden, Li Wenzie, Megg, Sugimura. According to a reporter from the New Life News Agency, a certain member of the committee said that today's meeting will discuss how to stabilize the prices of rice and flour and how to dredge the sources of foreign rice and wheat. Once a solution is decided, opinions on this issue will be submitted to the board of directors of the Municipal Council. The meeting notice has already been issued. The Shanghai Price Stabilization Committee has ordered another 20,000 bags of rice from Saigon for the fourth phase of price stabilization, in addition to the 15,000 bags previously stored. The cost of each bag (broken rice) is 54 yuan, excluding all expenses. Three-tenths of the deposit has been paid, totaling 324,000 yuan. The remaining 40,000 bags will be ordered as soon as the deposit is secured. After the additional 20,000 bags arrive in Shanghai around July 15, price stabilization will be launched. Yesterday, the Rice Industry Association and the Miscellaneous Grain Industry Association reiterated the previous order, restricting the weighing and clearing of rice and grain within ten days of the transaction.

The rice problem in this city has recently become serious again. Domestic rice has exceeded the 70 yuan mark, and foreign rice has also exceeded 60 yuan. The livelihood of the poor is worrying. The source of domestic rice is entirely controlled by the Japan-puppet regime. The amount of rice arriving in Shanghai every day cannot be investigated. The foreign rice is shipped from Saigon, Rangoon, Bangkok, and other ports in Vietnam. The soaring rice prices in this city are primarily due to the tightening of foreign exchange and the deliberate increase in prices. The Concession authorities had previously set a price limit of 40 yuan, but in reality, it has already been hovering around the 50 yuan mark. After holding on for several months, unexpectedly, the weather was extremely dry a few days ago, and the armistice between France and Germany caused rumors to spread in Vietnam, which gave speculators a great opportunity to spread rumors, saying that tribute rice could not be shipped to Shanghai and that the transshipment of foreign rice in Hong Kong was also prevented from being exported, etc., which repeatedly and drastically increased rice prices, creating unprecedented new prices. The livelihood of ordinary people cannot be maintained. According to reliable information from the shipping industry, the rice directly shipped from Saigon, Rangoon, and Siam has indeed been very little, but the rice shipped to Hong Kong for transshipment to Shanghai is continuous. Last week, Jardine Matheson & Co.'s Yisheng, Yisheng, and Lisheng lines shipped more than 51,400 sentences. On Saturday, the Taikoo Dockyard Company's Guangdong Wheel shipped 20,008 bags. On Sunday (the 23rd), the Xinjiang Wheel loaded another 11,774 bags, so the source will definitely not be interrupted. It is reported that the Java Company's Shibosha wheel is scheduled to ship rice directly from Saigon to Shanghai today. In addition, due to the recent rain, the five grains are expected to have a bumper harvest, and the old rice in the countryside is being milled one after another. Rice prices fell yesterday, but flour mills have increased their factory price to 14 yuan and 3 jiao.

The Rice Famine in Xiaoshao is Getting Worse; Xiangshan Reports Famine

The rice famine in Xiaoshao has been getting worse recently. The Xiaoshao Disaster Relief Association in this city received a telegram from the Shaoxing County Chamber of Commerce, Farmers' Association, Labor Union, Education Association, Women's Association, and other county-wide legal entities at 5:00 AM yesterday (the 24th), saying, "All of you are concerned about our homeland and have bestowed rescue. We are deeply grateful. The food famine has become more severe recently. In addition to doing our best to adjust and provide relief, we sincerely request that you quickly raise large sums of money for rescue. We are in dire straits." It is learned that the association has remitted 120,000 yuan to Shao yesterday and sent Wang Qingyun, Hong Wuqi, Chen Yinru, and others to purchase and distribute rice. It is also reported that the association is scheduled to hold a Xiaoshao Disaster Relief Fundraising Conference at the Shaoxing Seven Counties Association of Fellow Townsmen in Shanghai on Avenue Edward VII today. It is believed that the people of Shao are deeply concerned about their homeland and will definitely participate enthusiastically and donate large sums of money. In addition, the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Townsmen Association received an express mail from the Xiangshan County Government yesterday, saying, "Our county has never had enough rice, but we have been able to support ourselves by supplementing it with miscellaneous grains such as wheat, silk, etc. Last year's flood caused a disaster, and the late rice harvest was poor. It has been difficult to maintain the food supply for the entire county. However, neighboring counties, seeing that the prices in our county are lower, have come to purchase, resulting in a situation where supply cannot meet demand. Since the beginning of summer this year, the weather has been extremely dry, and the fields have cracked. About two-thirds of the early rice has not been sown in time. Even those that have been sown have withered seedlings, and it is difficult to expect a harvest. The disaster is already apparent. At present, there is no rice for sale, and tragic events of seizing grain, cutting off food, starving to death, and committing suicide are occurring frequently. According to investigations, Ru Yuyang Lai Aqiao in the west township committed suicide by drinking poisonous herbs because he had many family members, could not afford rice, and had no way to make a living. Zhou Songlai, a family of six in Xiangsi Ling in the east township, cut off food for three days, and his wife and children cried and screamed, secretly drinking brine and committing suicide. Sun Heding's family of five in Banana Sun in the west township cut off food for many days, and one son and one daughter starved to death one after another. Villagers in Zhuang Wu in Xisi Temple, Hutou in the east township, seized more than 100 jin of grain.

Tragic events are occurring frequently. Others, such as abandoning daughters and selling children, are unable to continue eating and prolong their lives by eating grass roots and bark. This is even more common everywhere. The severity of the food panic is actually greater than in the counties of Yong. We should ask your association to consider the people of Yong and provide relief to them as a whole, so as to relieve the disaster and appease our homeland. We are looking forward to it." It is heard that the association has telegraphed to Yong to request allocation.

Carrying Legal Tender to Border Provinces; Ban Cancelled; Travel from Kunming to Hong Kong, Shanghai, Tianjin and Other Places is Still Limited to 500 Yuan

The Ministry of Finance previously formulated measures to prevent the import of special goods by land, sea, and air in order to prevent capital flight and maintain the safety of the exchange market. It stipulated that the transport of gold and silver, gold and silver products, and banknotes to border provinces and borders, or the transport of such items from border provinces and borders to the interior, should be subject to strict restrictions. This measure was approved by the ministry and notified to travelers by the Executive Yuan. Subsequently, in order to strictly restrict the transport of banknotes, the Ministry of Finance separately formulated measures to restrict the export of banknotes, designating (1) that the transport of banknotes from Kunming to Hong Kong, or from the interior through Kunming, Hekou, Hong Kong, and other places to Shanghai, Tianjin, and other places, is limited to 500 yuan per person; (2) that the transport of banknotes from Hekou to Lao Cai should not exceed 20 yuan per person, and that the transport of banknotes from the interior through Hekou to Shanghai and other Chinese places is still limited to 500 yuan per person; (3) that the transport of banknotes from Tengchong to Bhamo is limited to 200 yuan per person; (4) that the transport of banknotes from Kunming or other places to Hekou is limited to 500 yuan; and (5) that the transport of legal tender abroad or to guerrilla areas from the interior is limited to Jiangbai yuan per person, except for those subject to special restrictions. This special project was also approved and telegraphed for implementation. Since the implementation of these measures, people have inevitably been restricted by these regulations when carrying legal tender to the hinterland. The closure will confine legal tender to a small corner. After careful verification, the Ministry of Finance believes that it is inconsistent with the meaning of the regulations and has made changes to the method of transporting banknotes. Except for the transport of gold and silver, gold and silver products, and banknotes out of the country, which should still be handled in accordance with the limited amount stipulated by the ministry, the transport of banknotes from the interior to various border provinces for circulation within the country, which does not involve export, should not be subject to restrictions on the amount, so that both the restriction on the export of legal tender and the need for circulation in various parts of the country can be taken into account. This changed method has been approved by the Executive Yuan and notified.

Lawyers Association Group Life Insurance; Lawyer Zhang Li's Opinion

The Shanghai Lawyers Association issued a circular to its members to solicit their approval of group life insurance and their opinions on the outline. According to lawyer Zhang Li's opinion, "I, as a member, am extremely in favor of the principle, but I dare not agree with the sentence 'death due to natural causes' in the first clause of the outline. (1) Everyone cherishes life and fears death. No one would attempt to commit suicide or arson for the sake of a thousand yuan insurance payout and equate such things with the same thing. Even if one is unfortunate enough to commit suicide, the pain is even greater than living in the world, and one has no choice but to resort to this last resort. One's situation is already pitiful. Why can't one be given compensation? In other cases, such as those who die in the line of duty (such as Judge Yu) or those who resist violence to the death, even if they are not members of this association, we should express our sympathy. How can we be members of this association, who have paid insurance premiums, and confiscate their insurance benefits? In order to prevent unscrupulous elements from being unworthy of death, this association should make arrangements in advance, or even refuse their insurance application to show restrictions. Therefore, according to my humble opinion, those who die should be given insurance benefits regardless of whether it is natural or accidental, in order to conform to the original intention of this association in handling life insurance."

The Rise and Fall of Things; The Traces of Prosperity and Decline are Fleeting; Continental Press Reporter's Impressions of Europe; Franco-German Armistice is Reciprocal Revenge; The Root of Future Disaster Has Already Been Conceived

When the news of the Franco-German armistice spread to Shanghai, Mr. Luo Xiaote, an editor of the Continental Press who had traveled in Europe for two and a half years, suddenly returned to Shanghai from the United States, resumed his duties at the office, and published his interesting text, saying, "When Hitler ordered the historic carriage in which the 1918 armistice was signed to be brought back to Berlin, he had already conceived the embryo of another war between Germany and France in the next 50 to 500 years. The French have a memory, and they will never forget anything. They will obtain compensation for any mistake before it is over. In this respect, the French have the spirit of the Chinese. In the past two years, I have traveled between Paris and Berlin, and I have often been filled with nostalgia.

The Palace of Versailles is Deserted

When we passed Versailles, we visited various places of historical interest and visited the Palace of Versailles. Although the palace was deserted, the paintings on the walls were hung as before, and no one dared to destroy them. Among them is the Hall of Mirrors, where the peace conference was held in 1919. The guards in the hall painstakingly pointed out and narrated to us which was the seat of US President Wilson and which were the seats of the German and French representatives.

The Franco-Prussian War was Signed Here

I was quite surprised why the peace conference of the European War was held in this empty and desolate Palace of Versailles instead of in Paris. I asked the guard, and the guard said, "I would like to tell you the reason. The reason why the peace conference was held in the Hall of Mirrors is that this is where the Prussian king forced us to end the Franco-Prussian War and sign the armistice in 1871."

The Same Dining Car; Old Drama Reenacted

He also told me that the long table where the peace conference was held was completely placed in its original place and had not been moved. Now, Hitler is forcing the French to make peace in the same dining car, because this car is where the French repelled the Germans in 1918. However, Mr. Xi is afraid that the French will repeat the old tune in the future and change their minds repeatedly, so he is preventing it in advance and taking the carriage back to Berlin.

German War Booty; The French Demand its Return

A few weeks ago, after visiting Paris, I returned to Berlin and met a German who was about to go to southeastern Germany to join a tank unit. I visited the Linden Memorial to Unknown Heroes with him, and on a platform near a fountain, I found an old-fashioned ammunition transport car. There was a copper plate on the car, and my friend translated its meaning, saying, "The guns on this car are war trophies obtained by the Prussian army in France in 1871. In 1919, at the time of the Paris peace conference, the French had requested the return of the guns, but they were especially preserved in this car. Now, when Hitler is in a whirlwind of activity, will this car in Linden still demand that the French return its guns? If so, then we can believe that in the next war, if the French win, they will definitely demand the return of their guns and empty cars to Paris."

Banks Engaging in Speculative Business; Ministry Orders Prohibition; Banks Should Set an Example; Employees Should Especially Abide by the Regulations

After the influx of floating capital into Shanghai, speculation has become rampant. It is heard that various commercial banks are using deposits to not only hoard goods but also buy foreign exchange with all their might, ostensibly "protecting deposits" but actually trying to make a fortune from the national crisis. Bank employees, from managers to trainees, are all engaged in speculation, competing to buy foreign exchange and hoard goods, causing social unrest. In addition, many bank employees are buying foreign exchange on behalf of their relatives and friends. Banks themselves and their employees were originally prohibited from engaging in speculative transactions. Now, after obtaining confidential information, the Ministry of Finance has strictly ordered an investigation and prohibition, and ordered that they refuse to underwrite the longest-term mortgages on daily necessities in order to avoid fueling speculation and affecting people's livelihood. Bank employees should abide by the regulations, and banks themselves should set an example in order to prevent malpractice.

Punishment of Unmarked Stalls Will Not Be Neglected

There has been a proposal to convert it into a floating hotel. However, due to the appropriate docking location not yet being determined, the aforementioned hotel conversion work has not yet commenced. Furthermore, the Italian expatriate population in this city is not large, totaling only about 650 people, residing in both concessions without any unrest. Although the Italian Consulate General has notified expatriates to restrain their behavior to avoid misunderstandings with British and French expatriates, the authorities in both concessions continue to provide protection to the Italian expatriates. Therefore, the Italian expatriates continue to reside as usual, and the relationships are extremely harmonious. Thus, relocating to ships is, in fact, unnecessary at present.

The Trade Commission has successively signed barter loan agreements with friendly nations, such as tea from the Soviet Union and tung oil and bristles from the United States. The commission pays off the barter goods and loans in full and on time, maintaining the country's external credit. It has won international praise. For example, because China can fulfill its obligations and deliver the goods as scheduled, American congressmen have proposed continuing loans to China. Therefore, the work of the commission, from the perspective of economic resistance, is indeed an important force, laying the economic foundation of the country.

Suspicious Case of Li Yuying's Sudden Death, Coffin Opened for Examination Yesterday, Hospital Authorities Conceal Report, Deceased's Parents Unaware

Li Yuying, also known as Li Jieru, daughter of Li Shizhen, a Fujianese elderly man in his seventies residing at No. 74, Lane 41, Tao'erfeisi Road in the French Concession, was 31 years old this year, had received higher education, and held celibacy. She had been the head nurse at the Sino-Western Sanatorium at No. 536 Pushi Road for six years. The director of the hospital, Lu Zhong'an, is from Beiping. Lu's son, Lu Zhenqing, 39 years old, serves as the office manager in the hospital. The hospital is a sanatorium, with both Chinese and Western doctors available to provide treatment according to the wishes of the patients. Because Li Yuying had worked in the hospital for a long time, she lived in the hospital, regarding it as her second home. She kept her savings, money, and clothing in the hospital and occasionally returned home to visit her parents. Her family are Christian believers. Li Yuying returned home on the evening of the Dragon Boat Festival this month to visit her parents, and returned to the hospital to sleep at night. When she said goodbye to her family at home, she was happy and showed no abnormality. Unexpectedly, Yuying returned to the hospital that night and died suddenly. It was not until 11 a.m. the next morning that Li Konglan, Li's niece, came to the hospital to give Yuying an injection. She knocked hard on the door and called out, but there was no response. After Lu Zhenqing, the hospital's office manager, took the key to open the door and enter the room, he discovered that Li Yuying had already died, and her body was cold. After discovering Li Yuying's sudden death, the hospital authorities notified the family members to come, but did not report it to the police according to the regulations of the concession hospital. Instead, Lu Zhenqing, the hospital's office manager, ordered the hospital's doctor, Lin Zhengliang, to be responsible for issuing a death certificate stating that Li Yuying died of apoplexy (stroke), and notified the Haige Road Chinese Funeral Home to transport the body to the funeral home. Lu Zhenqing, on behalf of the family, took out a portion of the funds from the deceased's savings to purchase high-quality Western-style clothing and a coffin, placed the body in the coffin, and temporarily placed the coffin in the funeral home. While searching for a burial site in the Hongqiao Cemetery and planning to bury the body on a selected date, a person

named Lei Huayun sent letters to the French Police Department, the Special Second Court, and the Fujianese Association in Shanghai, recounting the unclear death of Li Yuying and requesting justice and a thorough investigation to redress the grievances of the deceased. After receiving the letter, the French Police Department sent investigators to the Sino-Western Sanatorium and the Chinese Funeral Home to investigate. Both claimed that the deceased died of a stroke and had no definite evidence. Further investigation of the deceased's family did not reveal the cause of Li Yuying's death. Therefore, the police ordered the coffin to be sent to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall Examination Office for examination. Yesterday morning, the deceased's parents, Li Shizhen and Li Linshi, the office manager of the Sino-Western Sanatorium, Lu Zhenqing, the doctor Lin Zhengliang, and the staff of the Chinese Funeral Home who handled the matter were summoned to the case. Zhao Changmin, the prosecutor appointed by the Prosecutor's Office of the Special Second Court, and the forensic medical officer, etc., arrived at the autopsy site to open the coffin and examine the body. Because the Fujianese Association in Shanghai received a report from Lei Huayun, it sent Xu Shaoshan, the director of public relations of the association, to the scene to observe the examination. The worker

opened the coffin lid and took out the body for examination. The body had undergone surgery at the funeral home and had been given an antiseptic injection. The face turned black, and the skin and flesh of the whole body were tight and hard. External examination did not reveal the exact cause of death. The prosecutor asked Lin Zhengliang, who replied that he was a doctor at the Sino-Western Sanatorium, and he did not know the truth about the death of the deceased. Lu Zhenqing ordered me to issue a death certificate stating that she died of a stroke. When questioned Lu Zhenqing, he also prevaricated and shifted the responsibility to the family of the deceased. The deceased's father, Li Shizhen, said that he did not know the cause of his daughter's death at the time, and everything was handled by Lu Zhenqing. The deceased's mother, Li Linshi, said that her daughter left 6,700 yuan in cash and jewelry, all of which were in the hospital, and requested that they be returned. When questioned Lu Zhenqing, he said that the deceased had 7,000 yuan in cash, three gold bracelets, and more than 200 pieces of clothing of various styles stored in the hospital. He originally wanted to return them to the family of the deceased. According to a report from the investigators, the certificate signed by Dr. Lin is currently in the Health Department. According to the family of the deceased, Lu Zhenqing even promised the family to continue to pay the deceased's salary of 300 yuan per month. There is also a written request drafted by Lu Zhenqing for the family to ask the hospital to waive the autopsy, which is now in the hospital, etc. Zhao the prosecutor and the forensic doctor checked the confession and reprimanded Lu Lin for

concealing the sudden death of the person without reporting it to the police and for issuing a certificate randomly to the funeral home for burial. It was also suspected that the death of the deceased was suspicious and required a detailed investigation to make it clear and prevent any injustice. Therefore, the case was left for the police department to continue the investigation before further verification, or the body would be dissected for examination. Lu Zhenqing and Lin Zhengliang were suspected of being heavily responsible and were taken back to the police station by the investigators for investigation. The coffin will still be temporarily stored at the autopsy site, or it may need to be dissected for examination.

American Davis Robbed in Hongkou, Stops Rickshaw Puller, Robbed of 180 Yuan

Davis immediately shouted loudly to alert the police, but the "Avenue" police could not find any trace of them, so he went to the Jiaxing Road Police Station to report. However, it is not known what accent the bandits spoke, so it is not easy for the police to start the investigation.

A Certain Party Establishes a "Relief Association" to Manage Shanghai West Gambling Dens, the Property of Each Gambling Den Belongs to the "Association"

According to information obtained by the Shewen News Agency reporter, there is a very big reason for this, which is that a certain party reached an agreement with the gambling table owners to form a "Relief Association." The "Association" would send "staff" to be stationed in each gambling den to audit all expenses and supervise everything. The Female Boss of Huanlong Bathhouse Was Lured and Sold into Prostitution, Tricked of Huge Sums of Money and Defiled, Rogue Liang Lianqiao Punished and Fined

Mao Shoushan, a native of Danyang, has been running the Huanlong Bathhouse at No. 122 Huanlong Road in the French Concession. His business has been thriving recently, and he has accumulated a lot of wealth. His wife, Zhu, named Fengying, is 23 years old this year and has some beauty. She has been cohabiting with Mao. In April of this year, Zhu suddenly met Liang Lianqiao, a rogue from Jiangbei. They went to the Zhejiang Grand Theatre to watch a movie together. At that time, Liang learned that her family was wealthy, so he used his

silver tongue to lie that he had a steel factory in Tianjin with huge capital, and incited her to abandon her husband and run away with him to Tianjin to live a good life. Zhu was so bewitched by his sweet words that she not only had illicit relations with Liang at the Qinghe Hotel on Zhejiang Road that night, but also eloped with Liang on May 14, taking away her clothes and 5,000 yuan in cash. They met Liang at the Hu Ning Hotel on Jie Road and took the train to Tianjin together. They lived together at the Tianjin Hotel in Beikou for three days. Liang used his tricks to get all of Zhu's cash

, and sold her to Liu Shizhen's brothel in Shunde Li for 700 yuan to work as a prostitute. Liang took the money and returned to Shanghai, living comfortably in room 529 of the Oriental Hotel. Unexpectedly, the matter was discovered by the detectives of the Xinzha Police Station, who arrested Liang at the Oriental Hotel, seized 2,000 yuan in cash and a 1,000 yuan fixed deposit certificate from the Shanghai Bank, and took him to the police station. Yesterday morning, they sent Liang Lianqiao to the First Special Court Criminal Second Court along with Mao Shoushan, the husband of the victim. Zhang Tianyin, the lawyer of the police station,

filed a lawsuit according to law and detailed the above situation. According to Mao Shoushan's complaint, his wife recently borrowed 500 yuan from me on the pretext of her brother's wedding, and I gave her 5,000 yuan in legal currency to bring back because the price of farmland in the countryside was cheap. Unexpectedly, she eloped with someone. When Liang was questioned, he confessed everything. Judge Fu sentenced Liang to three years in prison for intending to lure women for profit, and fined him 500 yuan. If the fine is converted into labor service, it will be calculated at two yuan a day. A total of 3,000 yuan in legal currency and deposits seized will be returned to the original owner to receive it.

High Tide and Heavy Rain, Water Overflowing Roads, Related to Sewer Blockage

Although yesterday was still the high tide period after the full moon in the lunar calendar, the predicted quantity by the Dredging Bureau was only a little more than ten feet. However, at 2:30 p.m. yesterday, the actual quantity was above eleven feet. Coupled with the torrential rain, the sewers could not discharge the water in time, and the low-lying roads were flooded into canals. The deepest areas were in front of the Sincere Company on Nanjing Road, and the side of the company on Zhejiang Road, the side of Wing On Company at the south entrance of Nanjing Road, in front of the Times Theatre on Er Ma Road in Daxin Street, the north and south ends of Guangxi Road on Nanjing Road, Yinghua Street on Nanjing Road, the intersection of Jiujiang Road and Sichuan Road, the intersection of Hankou Road and Sichuan Road, the intersection of Alabashito Road and Gansu Road, the intersection of Fuxu Road and Chengdu Road, Sapo Sai Road, and the Bund, etc. The water accumulated to a foot deep in some places, and several inches deep in others, forming a watery world. The combination of high tide and heavy rain yesterday was the biggest reason for the road flooding. Secondly, the road could not discharge the water in time. However, the reason why the road cannot discharge the water in time is also related to the sewer blockage. The recent road flooding in Shanghai is always related to rain, and the recession is very slow, which can be clearly understood, which is not purely caused by the tide flowing backwards from the sewer.

Letter

To the Editor:

We are writing in response to the news item published on June 24 in the "Local News" section of your newspaper, concerning the "Da Fang Hotel's Occupation of Refugee Donations." The item states that the hotel industry has been collecting refugee donations from guests, but due to certain relationships, it has always allowed guests to donate voluntarily. To prevent malfeasance, it has been stated that any surplus amount remaining after settlement with the refugee association would be donated to other charities. This is not in accordance with the facts. This association has always collected refugee expenses from the hotel industry in accordance with the regulations, and has always collected and paid them in full. The Da Fang Hotel cannot be an exception. If the funds collected in the name of this association could be used freely by the collector, the malfeasance would be unimaginable. This letter is to request a correction in order to clarify the truth.

Sincerely,

Yuan Ludeng, Secretary General, Shanghai Refugee Relief Association, June 24

Old Newspaper Excerpts, Sixty-seven Years Ago (425) (See This Newspaper from the Twelfth Year of Tongzhi of the Late Qing Dynasty)

Bai Ge Piao (Pigeon Lottery)

Luzon is located in a remote part of the South Seas, a sparse collection of islands. The land is barren, the people are poor, and there are no local products to speak of. In terms of trade volume and the movement of goods by ship, it is like a small witch in the presence of a great wizard compared to other countries. However, its circulating Bai Ge Piao generates huge profits every month. Those involved in selling them say that the method is extremely fair. The drawings determine the winners and losers, with no private abuses. Moreover, all of this is done by the monarch himself, never delegated to others. Therefore, people everywhere win big prizes, but the people in that country are less likely to win, because the country has many poor people, making it difficult to afford tickets, and because the country is poor, there are few buyers. The surplus silver is used to support the widowed, orphaned, and lonely, making it a good law that uses wealth wisely, which is why it can last. Moreover, it can be expanded and extended. A few years ago, there were only 10,000 lottery numbers. Because there were not enough to sell, the number was increased to 12,000, and recently it has been increased to 13,000. In Shanghai alone, there are five sellers. In the past, people suspected that they were acting privately, but recently they have become deeply convinced and are competing to buy them. Initially, Westerners living there sold hundreds of tickets per month, but now Chinese people also sell hundreds of tickets. Those with more money buy the entire number, and those with less money buy half a ticket, or about several people buy it together, so more people win prizes. There are ten small lotteries and two large lotteries throughout the year. For the small lotteries, each ticket costs six yuan, and for the large lotteries, it costs twice as much. In Luzon, it only costs five or ten yuan, but in Shanghai, the ticket is marked up to cover water freight and the profits of the handler, so it is slightly more expensive.

To Be Published Tomorrow

The Author of Jin Ping Mei
