Free Talk

War

Concerning the Fifth Column

— Shi Tao

"Fifth Column," "Fifth Column," people all over the world are shuddering at this new term. Whether in Europe, Asia, or the Americas, whether in the belligerent or non-belligerent countries of the European war, this new type of spy army is lurking. England, France, Turkey, and other countries, in order to prevent its clandestine activities, have arrested many nationals and non-nationals. Even the United States, far across the ocean, has felt its terror and allocated $175,000 for the expenses of searching for the Fifth Column.

As early as five years ago, in 1936, when the Spanish revolutionary rebels advanced on Madrid, General Mola of Franco's headquarters announced: "Our army now has four columns of troops outside the city of Madrid, and there is also a Fifth Column lurking in the city. Madrid will be opened from within by their hands, so the capital will undoubtedly fall into our army's hands!"

This can be said to be the origin of the term "Fifth Column." During this European war, Germany used the Fifth Column to disrupt the enemy's internal affairs and collect enemy intelligence, etc., and achieved great success. This invisible spy army not only makes the enemy helpless, but also seems to disturb the peace of mind of the world. However, what kind of organization is the so-called Fifth Column after all? In short, the Fifth Column is the most elite spy army trained by Germany for this European war. It is, of course, under the command of Himmler, the head of the secret police. The number of people, tens of thousands, is naturally unknown. They all have to obey iron-like rules and accept instructions from the headquarters, adapting to circumstances in order to achieve the greatest effect, so the matter of "life" must be put aside. Among them are men, women, old, and young. In short, each is assigned the most appropriate job according to the difference in their origin and education.

Let's take an example. When Germany invaded Poland last year, on September 8, the Polish stronghold of R府市 was bombed by a large number of German aircraft. One of the planes was shot down by Polish fire, and two pilots were captured by the Polish army. Under interrogation, both were very young officers. Two years ago, these two had stayed in R府市 as students, and the leader of the two belonged to was also living in R府市 for a long time, engaged in commerce.

For example, during the invasion of the Netherlands, this group of Fifth Column personnel preemptively destroyed canals and bridges to hinder the Dutch military operations. They set fires in the enemy's gasoline storage depots, airfields, and shipyards, spread rumors, and disturbed people's minds, etc. These were all their methods of warfare.

The Fifth Column is not only made up of Germans, but also many powerful pro-German foreigners. With their power, they form even stronger organizations, scattered like cells in the country, carrying out activities. The success of the annexation of Austria by Germany is the best example. Even in countries that have not participated in the war, the activities of the Fifth Column are also extremely fierce. The Iron Guard in Romania implicitly opposed the King, first assassinating Prime Minister 加利南士哥, and then plotting to oppose the King. Recently, the King of Romania finally softened and had to ask to compromise with the group.

In this war, the German army has tried its best to propagate to France that Germany only hates Britain and has no reason to fight France, but the activity of the Fifth Column in France is really very harmful. President 某决勒幼仑 inspected the Alsace war line in great secrecy, and the German troops in front immediately raised a flag saying "Welcome to His Excellency the President of France," and the German broadcaster played "La Marseillaise." More interesting than this incident was when British Prime Minister Churchill and Eden inspected the French army and had lunch in Lille. This was of course a very secret matter, but when the two were seated, the radio on the table rang.

"This is the Berlin radio station. Now France is holding a luncheon for Ministers Churchill and Eden in Lille. Let me tell you the menu..."

Then, in fluent English, he accurately reported the current menu of the two ministers, without a single error. In France, no matter how big or small, Germany seems to be able to see everything at a glance, so it is no wonder that the impregnable Maginot Line was broken through by Germany.

The Fifth Column is simply ubiquitous and uses every trick. Whatever people can think of, it has already done it. Now that France has surrendered, this new type of "spy army" will overcome all obstacles and attack England and the Balkan countries!

Facts Speak Louder Than Words

— Lin Zhonghao

The progress of science, the development of transportation routes, and the prosperity of commerce have already made the countries of the world have an inextricably complex relationship. Therefore, it is impossible for a country to adopt an isolated and detached attitude and want to break away from the world and not be affected by world affairs.

When the Sino-Japanese war broke out, in addition to expressing great admiration and admiration for China's determination and perseverance in resisting the war, many foreigners were skeptical about the sentence "China is fighting for the safety of the world." Some even thought that it was purely a propaganda slogan for China to ask for foreign aid.

However, after the outbreak of the European war, facts finally speak louder than words. The Anglo-French allied forces suffered repeated defeats, and France even humiliatingly sought peace, almost without time to take care of the Far East. If China had not continued to resist bravely here, how the power of Britain and France in the Far East would have been devastated and hit, no one dared to predict.

"China is fighting for the world!" This is not an exaggeration, but a true fact!

Facts speak louder than words!

Cultivation

This is How a Person Should Be

— Written by Mead, Translated by Ku Kou

Respect my country, my profession, and myself. Treat my friends with honesty and justice, just as I want them to treat me with honesty and justice. Be a loyal citizen, praise my country, and do nothing to damage its reputation. Be a person whose reputation follows his name.

Base the hope of reward on service. Exchange success for honest effort. Always take work as an opportunity, happily seize it, and make the most of it. Do not regard it as a painful, reluctant, and forced servitude.

Remember that success lies in myself, in my own brainpower, in my own ambition, in my own courage and determination. When encountering difficulties, fight against them. Take the experience of hardship and difficulty as information for future work.

Be devoted to my profession. Make everyone I see optimistic. Dispel anger with happiness, eliminate suspicion with certainty, and reduce friction with people with an easygoing personality.

Study my business carefully. Know the various aspects of my profession in detail. Use both brain and strength, work systematically, and have a method. Do what must be done when I have free time, and do not waste time. Save time as a miser saves money. Make every hour generate interest, whether it is the increase of knowledge or the cultivation of body and mind.

Make my future not be burdened by debt. Earn money and save money. Give up all expensive entertainment until I can afford it. Abandon promiscuity, maintain the health of my body and the peace of mind, just like maintaining valuable inventory in trade.

Finally, hold on to the joy of life. Be a decent man in a bright and upright manner. Overcome my own weaknesses and strive to become a strong and superior person.

Then I can be courteous to others, loyal to friends, and have a clear conscience before heaven.

The Trajectory of Life

— Tie Ren

The road of "wait a little while" will lead to the room of "never." —— Cervantes

A person who is tired of his own life completely does not understand the meaning of life. —— Thoreau

A true warrior dares to face the bleak life, dares to face the dripping blood. —— Lu Xun

Wealth and luxury may not be able to satisfy a person. At least, I know that wealthy people cannot accomplish anything of value. —— Duncan

Words are temporary things, but silence is eternal. —— Maeterlinck

Entertainment Circle

Kunming Film Industry Overview

— Qian

(Kunming Airlines News) A year ago, in the summer, I arrived in Kunming, as if I had walked into a desert. When friends met, the methods to find entertainment in spirit were nothing more than playing chess, or trying their luck, acting on the spot, and playing mahjong to pass the time.

This is the same as the situation in the American West during its development. Now, this city is becoming more and more prosperous day by day! In the southern district of Kunming, among many beautiful buildings, a giant theater has emerged, which is the Nanping Grand Theater. It meets all reasonable requirements, has the beauty of both classic and modern times, is solemn and magnificent, and more valuable, the projection machine is a "Peacock Brand" automatic and complete instrument, for a blockbuster, it delicately and accurately shows it to the audience; until now, it has introduced a first-class blockbuster to the people of Kunming. This is:

Wings Over the World (Paramount). Stooges Go West (MGM). Bitter Sweet (United Artists). Virginia City (Warner Bros.). The Cowboy and the Lady (United Artists). The Oppenheim Family (Soviet Union). The Firefly (United Artists). If I Were King (Paramount). Little Lord Fauntleroy (United Artists). Camille (United Artists).

On the day of its birth on April 2nd of this year, facing the Nanping Grand Theater from afar, a music hall was being built, which was the prototype of the New Dayi Amusement Cinema. It was established with an investment of 300,000 yuan, because its shareholders are part of the shareholders of the Nanping Theater. In the Kunming film industry, they are sister theaters. In addition to the sisters, there are also a pair of old brothers, called the Dazhong Cinema and the Old Dayi Amusement Cinema. The perfection of the equipment and the strictness of the film selection are not worth mentioning. Their business policy is to entertain the audience with low-cost tickets. This may be unique here. During the screening, staff members tell the story of the play and the lines on the stage. Most of the Kunming audience believes that explaining the plot can increase the interest in watching the play.

The number of times that domestic films are shown here is very small. - Mysterious Flower, Isolated Island Paradise, and Northern Battlefield Loyal Record are like a flash in the pan. Recently, China Film Corporation shot the exterior scenes of "Thousands of Miles in the Air" in Kunming, and also brought many excellent actors, which made everyone pay attention to domestic films. I very much hope that the Shanghai film company will jointly set up a joint office in Kunming to introduce domestic films to the audience in the mainland as much as possible.

The development of Kunming's film industry proves that this city is progressing, at least it is no longer a desert! (Sent on June 15th)

Spoken Drama Su Wu Shepherding

— Zou Xiao

It is said that the United Arts Experimental Troupe and the professional troupe of Chu Xinxing are organized by ambitious young people, which is very admirable. This performance of Wang Jixu's creation "Su Wu Shepherding" is still the first public performance.

This play is mostly in line with historical facts, that is, Su Wu's son Tong Guo is also in the official history. Han Shu Volume 54 Su Jianzi Wu Biography Yun: "When Wu was old, his son died before he was seated. The emperor felt sorry for him; he asked the people around him whether Wu had a son in the Xiongnu? Wu Bai Bai Yin Ping Enhou himself said that when he sent the Xiongnu, a son Tong Guo was born to the Hu woman. There were voices asking to use the envoy to send gold and silk to redeem him. The emperor allowed it. Later, Tong Guo followed the envoy, and the emperor thought he was a Lang. It's just that I didn't mention whether the Hu woman would return home with him. Lake Baikal is Lake Baihaer. Historical Records Note Yun: "The North Sea is the northern border of the Xiongnu, and now it is Lake Baihaer."

Guo Moruo once wrote several poems in "Electric Light and Flint," one of which was Su Wu Shepherding. Now this spoken drama is also a beautiful long poem. Because of the design of Hu Xuguang, Ling Lei, etc., and the director of Wu Yonggang, etc., each scene has many beautiful pictures, and the position of the characters is also very beautiful. Although it is just a piece of white cloth covering the mountain, and two real sheep are tied to the fence, it is very much like a snowy and icy world; the costumes are also completely different from Peking Opera and Kunqu Opera, purely Han Dynasty clothing, I think Ma Lianliang may also refer to it. As for the actors, Tie Nuo's Su Wu is the most successful. Xiao Qing's Tong Guo is also very cute, but the word "Jiang" in surrender should be read in the first tone, but it was mistakenly read in the fourth tone.

It is unexpected that such a calm subject matter can be performed actively and lively, from beginning to end, and the audience does not feel tired.

Tong Guo recognizes the words on the sand, and Su Wu gives his son the wind hat before returning home. These are all very poetic. The play writes about the loyalty and bravery of Su Wu and Chang Hui, which is contrasted with Wei Lu and Zhang Sheng, etc., which is the main theme of the play. The success of this point has been confirmed by the popularity of the box office in recent days.

(Left) Ms. Lu Shan, the heroine of Su Wu Shepherding (Right) A glimpse of the stage

— Photo by Yang Jianzhang

Inland Film and Drama

— Chan

Shen Xiling left China Film Corporation last month and joined China Film Studio.

China Film Studio recently sent Zheng Junli to Xichang to shoot films about the customs of the Yi people.

Ms. Fengzi, the editor of the "Pingming" supplement of the Central Daily News, is shooting "The Frontier Storm" in Chongqing, which has now been completed. She plays the wife of Bai Kanshi.

Ouyang Yuqian is rehearsing "Mulan Joins the Army," "Victory Year," "The Peach Blossom Fan," "Peach Blossom Face," and "Rebellion" in Guilin, which are selling very well.

Tian Ao completed the entire script of "Yue Fei" last month, with a total length of 50,000 words, which was published in the Changsha National Daily.

Impressions of "The Net of Heaven and Earth"

— Shen Qi

The performance of "The Net of Heaven and Earth," although containing a kind of preaching meaning of "cause and effect" retribution, forcefully emphasizes a kind of psychological punishment and satirizes the irregular life of general collapsing strata.

Reviewing the play "The Net of Heaven and Earth," the progress of the story is very simple, explaining that after a person commits a crime, it is equivalent to owing a debt to society. Even if it is suspended or even avoided, it must be repaid in the end. The structure of the whole play is tense and exciting, with many climaxes surging in the five acts and eleven scenes. The murder of Mei Jieying by Ma Yuchuan in the second act, and the departure of Na Ru and the suicide of A Nan in the fourth act, etc., can all suppress the audience's emotions. The satire is also very strong.

As for the performance, Zhou Chu's Ma Jinchuan is the most important and the most successful in the whole play. The inner conflict of love and hate is fully displayed, especially in the movements, he can always enhance the terrifying scene, and the tone and tone are also enough to show a kind of, sick, and frivolous personality, which is also in line with his identity. A Nan is a sincere and simple person with the image of a good wife and mother in the play. Zhang Xuemei's performance is very vivid. Qiu Quan's Hai Meng and Lan Qing's Mrs. Grant are very competent, using fluent spoken language to set off their expressions. The rest, Mei Jieying of the Yellow River, and the doctor of Shao Hua, although they appear less, they have worked hard in drama and art.

Finally, after watching the whole play, I feel that we don't have to hate people, let alone hate criminals. What we hate is the social system. At the same time, we should work hard to reform the old system and create a new world!

Thoughts After Watching "Yang Paifeng"

— Lu Yuan Scholar

Shi Shan has performed the play "Yang Paifeng" (originally named "Fire Stick Performance") at the Renewal Stage for five or six times. Every performance is full, which shows his appeal. I was able to take the time to watch it the other night. The whole play is full and impeccable, and it is indeed a good structure. The reputation is by no means accidental. In short, Shi Shan's art can be summarized by the four words of vigorous and steady. As for the beauty of his posture and the lightness of his style, what is called flying like a startled goose and swimming like a dragon is especially superfluous.

According to this play, it should be simply called "Four Fights." There are many examples in dramas such as the Three Visits, Three Searches, and Three Slashes, and there is also a play called "Three Fights" in front (Yao Gang fights Wang Ying), so it is even more possible to name it "Four Fights." After watching, I wrote two poems:

After Qinglong fights, he fights Jiao Meng, internal strength succeeds in resisting foreign countries; the fire girl has many war achievements, and even sees Han Chang fighting in battle.

I only see the hand spinning like a wheel, the head-on blow is like waving a whip; the Hu children are strong and useless, kneeling before the heroine of Shenzhou.

New Lineups of the Two Drama Circles (Below)

— Only Me

Clown Ci Ruiquan, is a senior clown, and is also a typical figure in the Liyuan today. He has been paired with the Tan family for generations. His qualifications, experience, reputation, and status are similar to Xiao Changhua. Due to his age, he has not been here for a long time. (Old Ci is a basic figure in the Cheng Yanqiu and Tan Fuying classes, but in the past Yanqiu came south, Old Ci did not follow him, and his son Shaoquan acted as a substitute, that is, when Fuying came to Shanghai last time, he also changed to invite Ru Fuhui because Old Ci was unwilling to suffer from the boat). This time, he resolutely went south, and we were able to see the typical figure of the senior, which can be said to be a great blessing. There is also Luo Wenkui, a famous clown in the north. Shanghai people are not very familiar with him, so it is necessary to introduce him: This person is the son of the old actor Luo Baisui. He has a family background and his art is quite extraordinary. Unfortunately, he was not met when he was young. In recent years, he has been teaching students in Ping, and he has never been in class. He has been quite frustrated. This time, he can be invited by Fuying, which can be said to be a Maxima meeting Bole. Wu Xing Zhang Lianting, is invited by Yang Shengchun's helper. According to Shengchun's helper, Han Shengxin was originally Shengchun's helper. This time Shengchun came south without inviting Shengxin, but invited Lianting, (according to Zhang Lianting is Gao Shenglin's helper) is also a strange thing. Hua Dan Ji Yanfen, originally named Xiao Guihua, is a disciple of Binqing Society, and is a teacher brother with Gu Yulan of the current Renewal Stage, (according to Gu Yulan's original name is Yulan Hua) was very popular in the early years, but now he is old and fading. The old Sheng Ha Baoshan, is a rising star. His art is no less than that of the predecessor Zhang Chunyan, and he is also a rich old partner. Song Jiting is also commendable. Looking at the supporting roles invited by Fuying this time, we can call them "a gathering of talents." What can be described even more is that many of the supporting roles here are relatives of the Tan family, such as Yang Shengchun is Fuying's sister Qian, Jiang Miaoxiang is Taiying's Taishan, Tan Shiying is Fuying's brother, and Song Jiting is Fuying's brother-in-law, etc. (Fuying's ex-wife is the Song family) This can also be said to be that internal promotion does not avoid relatives, and their performances are often more like a raging fire. One laugh.

Latest news: Regarding the Tan Troupe invited by the Renewal Stage, there are slight changes in the personnel. The painted face Ma Liankun did not reach an agreement due to official business issues and has stopped coming south. The old actor Ci Ruiquan decided to accompany Tan. In addition, there is one thing that the reporter did not expect, that is, Wu Sheng Yang Shengchun's target Han Shengxin decided to come with Shengchun, and Zhang Lianting was also on the list of invitees. It is also learned that Tan Fuying will come to Shanghai to perform the play "Silang Visits His Mother". The Tan Troupe has re-invited the old Dan He Shengqing (Fucheng Fourth Branch has two old Dan talents, one is Li Shengquan and the other is He Shengqing) to join, adding to the strength. The strength of this group of people in the Renewal Stage has become more and more strong.
